Your role in this election drama is over, but your legacy, your fight for America’s soul, will carry on.

let regex = new RegExp('(^|[^A-Za-z0-9])(' + searchString + ')(?=$|[^A-Za-z0-9])', 'gi'); let match; while ((match = regex.exec(str)) !== null) { let start = match.index + match[1].length; let end = start + match[2].length; matches.push({ start: start, end: end, tooltipIndex: index }); } }); matches.sort((a, b) => a.start - b.start || b.end - b.start - (a.end - a.start)); for (let i = 0; i < matches.length - 1; ) { if (matches[i + 1].start < matches[i].end) { matches.splice(i + 1, 1); } else { i++; } } return matches; } function applyTooltips(str) { if (typeof str !== 'string' || str.indexOf('mytooltip') !== -1) { return str; } const matches = getTooltips(str); let result = ''; let lastIndex = 0; lastIndex = match.end; }); result += str.slice(lastIndex); return result; } function applyTooltipsToObject(obj) { for (let key in obj) { if (typeof obj[key] === 'string') { obj[key] = applyTooltips(obj[key]);
